ALTER TABLE [dbo].[Accounts] ADD  CONSTRAINT [uqaccount] UNIQUE NONCLUSTERED 
(
	[Account] ASC
)WITH (PAD_INDEX = OFF, STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE = OFF, SORT_IN_TEMPDB = OFF, IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF, ONLINE = OFF, ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS = ON, ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS = ON) ON [PRIMARY]
GO
ALTER TABLE [dbo].[AccountTransactions]  WITH CHECK ADD  CONSTRAINT [fkacno] FOREIGN KEY([Accno])
REFERENCES [dbo].[Customers] ([Accno])
GO
ALTER TABLE [dbo].[AccountTransactions] CHECK CONSTRAINT [fkacno]
GO
ALTER TABLE [dbo].[Customers]  WITH NOCHECK ADD  CONSTRAINT [fkAccounts] FOREIGN KEY([Account])
REFERENCES [dbo].[Accounts] ([Id])
GO
ALTER TABLE [dbo].[Customers] CHECK CONSTRAINT [fkAccounts]
GO
ALTER TABLE [dbo].[AccountTransactions]  WITH CHECK ADD  CONSTRAINT [chkttype] CHECK  (([ttype]=(2) OR [ttype]=(1)))
GO
ALTER TABLE [dbo].[AccountTransactions] CHECK CONSTRAINT [chkttype]
GO
ALTER TABLE [dbo].[Customers]  WITH NOCHECK ADD  CONSTRAINT [ckhststua] CHECK  (([status]=(1) OR [status]=(0)))
GO
ALTER TABLE [dbo].[Customers] CHECK CONSTRAINT [ckhststua]
